0"></path><path d="M19.98 10.023c0 .2-.058.399-.168.547l-4.996 7.492a.987.987 0 01-.828.454h-3c-.547 0-.996-.453-.996-1 0-.2.059-.403.168-.551l4.625-6.942-4.625-6.945a.939.939 0 01-.168-.55 1 1 0 01.996-.997h3c.348 0 .649.18.828.45l4.996 7.492c.11.148.168.347.168.55zm0 0"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></aside><main class="docMainContainer_TBSr"><div class="container padding-top--md padding-bottom--lg"><div class="row"><div class="col docItemCol_z5aJ"><div class="docItemContainer_c0TR"><article><nav class="theme-doc-breadcrumbs breadcrumbsContainer_Z_bl" aria-label="Breadcrumbs"><ul class="breadcrumbs"><li class="breadcrumbs__item"><a class="breadcrumbs__link" href="/weaviate/manage-collections"><span>How-to: Manage collections</span></a></li><li class="breadcrumbs__item breadcrumbs__item--active"><span class="breadcrumbs__link">Migrate data</span></li></ul></nav><div class="tocCollapsible_ETCw theme-doc-toc-mobile tocMobile_ITEo"><button type="button" class="clean-btn tocCollapsibleButton_TO0P">On this page</button></div><div class="theme-doc-markdown markdown"><header><h1>Migrate data</h1></header><p>Follow these examples to migrate data manually when using a backup is not possible. They cover all permutations between:</p>
<ul>
<li class="">a single-tenancy collection (Collection), and</li>
<li class="">a tenant in a multi-tenancy collection (Tenant).</li>
</ul>
<details class="details_lb9f alert alert--info details_b_Ee" data-collapsed="true"><summary>Additional information</summary><div><div class="collapsibleContent_i85q"><p>The examples use two different Weaviate instances, exposed through different ports. The same process can be used for two different instances as well.</p><p>Cross-references in Weaviate are properties. As such, you can <a class="" href="/weaviate/manage-collections/cross-references#read-cross-references">retrieve cross-reference</a> as a part of the object.</p></div></div></details>
<details class="details_lb9f alert alert--info details_b_Ee" data-collapsed="true"><summary>What about cross-references?</summary><div><div class="collapsibleContent_i85q"><p>These scripts should migrate cross-references as well.</p><br><p>Cross-references are properties. As such, these cursor-based exports will include them.
During restoration, restore the cross-referenced (i.e. &quot;to&quot;) object first, then the object that contains the cross-reference (i.e. &quot;from&quot; object).</p></div></div></details>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="collection--collection">Collection → Collection<a href="#collection--collection" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Collection → Collection" title="Direct link to Collection → Collection" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="step-1-create-the-target-collections">Step 1: Create the target collection(s)<a href="#step-1-create-the-target-collections" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Step 1: Create the target collection(s)" title="Direct link to Step 1: Create the target collection(s)" translate="no">​</a></h4>
<p>Create a collection (e.g. <code>WineReview</code>) at the target instance, matching the collection (e.g. <code>WineReview</code>) at the source instance.</p>

<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="step-2-migrate-the-data">Step 2: Migrate the data<a href="#step-2-migrate-the-data" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Step 2: Migrate the data" title="Direct link to Step 2: Migrate the data" translate="no">​</a></h4>
<p>Migrate:</p>
<ul>
<li class="">The <code>source collection</code> data in the <code>client_src</code> instance</li>
<li class="">to <code>target collection</code> in the <code>client_tgt</code> instance</li>
</ul>

<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="collection--tenant">Collection → Tenant<a href="#collection--tenant" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Collection → Tenant" title="Direct link to Collection → Tenant" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="step-1-create-the-target-collections-1">Step 1: Create the target collection(s)<a href="#step-1-create-the-target-collections-1" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Step 1: Create the target collection(s)" title="Direct link to Step 1: Create the target collection(s)" translate="no">​</a></h4>
<p>Create a collection (e.g. <code>WineReview</code>) at the target instance, matching the collection (e.g. <code>WineReview</code>) at the source instance, and enable multi-tenancy for the target collection.</p>

<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="step-2-create-the-tenants">Step 2: Create the tenant(s)<a href="#step-2-create-the-tenants" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Step 2: Create the tenant(s)" title="Direct link to Step 2: Create the tenant(s)" translate="no">​</a></h4>

<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="step-3-migrate-the-data">Step 3: Migrate the data<a href="#step-3-migrate-the-data" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Step 3: Migrate the data" title="Direct link to Step 3: Migrate the data" translate="no">​</a></h4>
<p>Migrate:</p>
<ul>
<li class="">The <code>source collection</code> data in the <code>client_src</code> instance</li>
<li class="">to <code>target tenant</code> data from <code>target collection</code> in the <code>client_tgt</code> instance</li>
</ul>

<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="tenant--collection">Tenant → Collection<a href="#tenant--collection" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Tenant → Collection" title="Direct link to Tenant → Collection" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="step-1-create-the-target-collections-2">Step 1: Create the target collection(s)<a href="#step-1-create-the-target-collections-2" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Step 1: Create the target collection(s)" title="Direct link to Step 1: Create the target collection(s)" translate="no">​</a></h4>
<p>Create a collection (e.g. <code>WineReview</code>) at the target instance, matching the collection (e.g. <code>WineReview</code>) at the source instance, and enable multi-tenancy for the target collection.</p>

<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="step-2-migrate-the-data-1">Step 2: Migrate the data<a href="#step-2-migrate-the-data-1" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Step 2: Migrate the data" title="Direct link to Step 2: Migrate the data" translate="no">​</a></h4>
<p>Migrate:</p>
<ul>
<li class="">The <code>source tenant</code> data from <code>source collection</code> in the <code>client_src</code> instance</li>
<li class="">to <code>target collection</code> in the <code>client_tgt</code> instance</li>
</ul>

<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="tenant--tenant">Tenant → Tenant<a href="#tenant--tenant" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Tenant → Tenant" title="Direct link to Tenant → Tenant" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="step-1-create-the-target-collections-3">Step 1: Create the target collection(s)<a href="#step-1-create-the-target-collections-3" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Step 1: Create the target collection(s)" title="Direct link to Step 1: Create the target collection(s)" translate="no">​</a></h4>
<p>Create a collection (e.g. <code>WineReview</code>) at the target instance, matching the collection (e.g. <code>WineReview</code>) at the source instance including enabling multi-tenancy.</p>

<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="step-2-create-the-tenants-1">Step 2: Create the tenant(s)<a href="#step-2-create-the-tenants-1" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Step 2: Create the tenant(s)" title="Direct link to Step 2: Create the tenant(s)" translate="no">​</a></h4>

<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="step-3-migrate-the-data-1">Step 3: Migrate the data<a href="#step-3-migrate-the-data-1" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Step 3: Migrate the data" title="Direct link to Step 3: Migrate the data" translate="no">​</a></h4>
<p>Migrate:</p>
<ul>
<li class="">The <code>source tenant</code> data from <code>source collection</code> in the <code>client_src</code> instance</li>
<li class="">to <code>target tenant</code> data from <code>target collection</code> in the <code>client_tgt</code> instance</li>
</ul>
